Task instruction sent to agent 
# Kafka Consumer Fetch Request to Record Processing Chain

## Your Task

Trace how a Kafka consumer fetch request is built, sent, and processed back into ConsumerRecords in apache/kafka. Find Java source files implementing: the Fetcher request builder, the network poll, the fetch response parsing, and the ConsumerRecords population.

## Context

You are working on a codebase task involving repos from the crossrepo tracing domain.

## Available Resources

The local `/workspace/` directory contains: sg-evals/kafka--0753c489, sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc, sg-evals/camel--1006f047.

**Note:** Additional repositories are accessible via Sourcegraph MCP tools:
- `sg-evals/kafka--0753c489` (apache/kafka)
- `sg-evals/flink--0cc95fcc` (apache/flink)
- `sg-evals/camel--1006f047` (apache/camel)

## Output Format

Create a file at `/workspace/answer.json` with your findings in the following structure:

```json
{
  "files": [
    {"repo": "org/repo-name", "path": "relative/path/to/file.go"}
  ],
  "symbols": [

}
```

Include only the fields relevant to this task. Your answer is evaluated against a closed-world oracle — completeness matters.

- **File recall and precision**: Did you find all relevant files?

Perfect! I've created a comprehensive trace of the Kafka consumer fetch request processing chain. Here's a summary of what I found:

## Kafka Fetch Request Processing Chain

The chain encompasses **10 key Java files** implementing the complete fetch lifecycle:

### Request Building Phase
- **FetchRequestManager.createFetchRequests()** - Creates fetch requests based on subscription state
- **AbstractFetch.prepareFetchRequests()** - Prepares request data per node
- **AbstractFetch.createFetchRequest()** - Builds the actual FetchRequest.Builder

### Request Transmission Phase  
- **Fetcher.sendFetches()** - Sends requests to brokers
- **ConsumerNetworkClient.send()** - Network layer communication

### Response Parsing Phase
- **AbstractFetch.handleFetchSuccess()** - Processes FetchResponse objects
- **FetchBuffer.add()** - Stores CompletedFetch objects (partition batch results)

### Record Collection Phase
- **FetchCollector.collectFetch()** - Main collector method iterating through buffered fetches
- **CompletedFetch.fetchRecords()** - Deserializes record batches into ConsumerRecord objects
- **Fetch** - Intermediate aggregator of records by partition
- **ConsumerRecords** - Final user-facing container with Map<TopicPartition, List<ConsumerRecord>>

All findings have been written to `/workspace/answer.json` with complete file paths, method symbols, and a detailed narrative explaining the complete processing flow.
